<p><b>Pierre-Emerick Emiliano François Aubameyang</b> (born 18 June 1989) is a Gabonese professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Striker_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Striker (association football)">striker</a> and is the <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> of both <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Gabon_national_football_team" title="Gabon national football team">Gabon national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Renowned for his pace, finishing, and off-ball movement,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> his former manager, <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klopp" title="Jürgen Klopp">Jürgen Klopp</a>, considered Aubameyang to be one of the best forwards in world football.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The son of former Gabonese international <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Aubameyang" title="Pierre Aubameyang">Pierre Aubameyang</a>, Pierre-Emerick began his senior club career playing for Italian club <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a>, but never appeared for the club as he went on a series of <a href="/wiki/Loan_(sports)" title="Loan (sports)">loan</a> spells in France. He moved to <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> in 2011. There, he won a <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="2012–13 Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> title and joined <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> in 2013. In Germany, Aubameyang finished as the league's <a href="/wiki/List_of_Bundesliga_top_scorers" title="List of Bundesliga top scorers">top goalscorer</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Bundesliga" title="2016–17 Bundesliga">2016–17 season</a> and won a <a href="/wiki/2017_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2017 DFB-Pokal Final">DFB-Pokal</a>. He also ranks as the club's sixth highest <a href="/wiki/List_of_Borussia_Dortmund_players#All-time_top_10_goalscorers" title="List of Borussia Dortmund players">all-time</a> goalscorer.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Aubameyang was the subject of a then-club <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">record association football transfer</a> when signed for Arsenal in a <a href="/wiki/Transfer_(association_football)" title="Transfer (association football)">transfer</a> worth £56 million (€60 million), making him the most expensive Gabonese player of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> With Arsenal, Aubameyang won a <a href="/wiki/2020_FA_Cup_Final" title="2020 FA Cup Final">FA Cup</a> and finished as the league's joint-<a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Golden_Boot" title="Premier League Golden Boot">top goalscorer</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Premier_League" title="2018–19 Premier League">2018–19 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang ranks as Gabon's <a href="/wiki/Gabon_national_football_team#Records" title="Gabon national football team">all-time top goalscorer</a>. He made his senior debut for Gabon in 2009 aged 19, and appeared in three <a href="/wiki/Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="Africa Cup of Nations">Africa Cup of Nations</a> tournaments, as well as the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2012 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2012 Summer Olympics</a>. For his performances at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">2015 Africa Cup of Nations</a>, Aubameyang was named <a href="/wiki/African_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="African Footballer of the Year">African Footballer of the Year</a>, becoming the first Gabonese player, and second-European born player, to win the award.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="A.C._Milan">A.C. Milan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: A.C. Milan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"My role model? <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>. I think he has revolutionised football with his way of playing. He was dynamic, technically strong and fast. He was an enormous player."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Aubameyang on the influence of his idol, Brazilian striker Ronaldo, on his own career.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Aubameyang joined <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a>'s youth academy in January 2007. In August, he was part of the squad that finished fourth in the <a href="/wiki/2007_Champions_Youth_Cup" title="2007 Champions Youth Cup">inaugural Champions Youth Cup</a> held in Malaysia, where he made a name for himself and attracted the attention of scouts internationally. He scored against every opponent Milan played, finishing with seven goals in six matches.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2008.E2.80.9309:_Loan_to_Dijon"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2008–09:_Loan_to_Dijon">2008–09: Loan to Dijon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2008–09: Loan to Dijon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Ligue_1" title="2008–09 Ligue 1">2008–09 season</a>, Aubameyang was loaned out to <a href="/wiki/Dijon_FCO" title="Dijon FCO">Dijon</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ligue_2" title="Ligue 2">Ligue 2</a> in France to gain first team experience.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> His performances there led him to appear in <i><a href="/wiki/World_Soccer_(magazine)" title="World Soccer (magazine)">World Soccer's</a></i> Talent Scout section in Summer 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He finished with a total of ten goals and two assists in all competitions, including two goals in a <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a> tie against <a href="/wiki/Is-Selongey_Football" title="Is-Selongey Football">Selongey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2009.E2.80.9310:_Loan_to_Lille"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2009–10:_Loan_to_Lille">2009–10: Loan to Lille</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 2009–10: Loan to Lille">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 24 June 2009, it was announced <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a> had decided to sign Aubameyang on loan.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Relative to his previous season, however, Aubameyang did not perform as well, scoring just two goals in 14 appearances, four as a starter.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311:_Loans_to_Monaco_and_Saint-.C3.89tienne"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–11:_Loans_to_Monaco_and_Saint-Étienne">2010–11: Loans to Monaco and Saint-Étienne</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2010–11: Loans to Monaco and Saint-Étienne">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_AS_Monaco_FC_season" title="2010–11 AS Monaco FC season">2010–11 season</a>, Aubameyang was loaned for the season to <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>. On 21 August 2010, he scored his first goal for Monaco in an away match against <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a>, then scored again on 29 August at home to <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a>, where Monaco won 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> In January 2011, after six months with the club, Aubameyang was loaned to <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> until the end of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Ligue_1" title="2010–11 Ligue 1">2010–11 season</a>, finishing the season with four goals and three assists. In July 2011, the loan was extended for the entire <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Ligue_1" title="2011–12 Ligue 1">2011–12 season</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Saint-.C3.89tienne"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Saint-Étienne">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_(03-08-2011).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg/170px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg/255px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg/340px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%2803-08-2011%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1750" data-file-height="2625" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_(03-08-2011).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang at <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 December 2011, Aubameyang signed with Saint-Étienne on a permanent deal. He was quickly added to the starting line up and was given the number 7 jersey. In February 2012, he scored his first <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Lorient" title="FC Lorient">Lorient</a>. He became an integral part of the squad, scoring half of the team's away goals during the season, and went on to be Ligue 1's top goalscorer with 16 goals.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 20 April 2013, Aubameyang was in the starting line-up for Saint-Étienne in the <a href="/wiki/2013_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2013 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2013 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>. <i>Les Verts</i> won the match 1–0 with a goal from <a href="/wiki/Brand%C3%A3o_(footballer,_born_1980)" title="Brandão (footballer, born 1980)">Brandão</a> to give Aubameyang his first major trophy as a professional footballer. He finished the season with 18 goals and seven assists in all competitions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Ligue_1" title="2012–13 Ligue 1">2012–13 season</a>, Aubameyang ended second in the competition's <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Ligue_1#Top_goalscorers" title="2012–13 Ligue 1">top-goalscorers list</a>, scoring 19 goals and finishing behind only <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a>. From his 37 appearances, he also provided eight <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Ligue_1#Assists_table" title="2012–13 Ligue 1">assists</a>. The season was widely regarded as his breakout year—he appeared in the Ligue 1 team of the season and he won the Ligue 1 African Player of the Year award.<sup id="cite_ref-Ligue_1_Best_African_Player_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ligue_1_Best_African_Player-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Borussia_Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Borussia Dortmund">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314:_DFL-Supercup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14:_DFL-Supercup">2013–14: DFL-Supercup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2013–14: DFL-Supercup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg/170px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg" decoding="async" width="170" height="285" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg/255px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg/340px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="498" data-file-height="835" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_2013.jpeg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang with <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>On 4 July 2013, Aubameyang joined <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2013 UEFA Champions League Final">2012–13 Champions League finalists</a> <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> on a five-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He made his competitive debut for his new club on 27 July 2013 against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2013_DFL-Supercup" title="2013 DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercup</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Jakub_B%C5%82aszczykowski" title="Jakub Baszczykowski">Jakub Baszczykowski</a> for the last 18 minutes of Dortmund's 4–2 victory, assisting Dortmund's final goal, scored by <a href="/wiki/Marco_Reus" title="Marco Reus">Marco Reus</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> On 10 August, Aubameyang made his <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> debut and scored a hat-trick against <a href="/wiki/FC_Augsburg" title="FC Augsburg">FC Augsburg</a>, including a goal from his first <a href="/wiki/Shooting_(association_football)" title="Shooting (association football)">shot</a> in the league. In the process, Aubameyang also became the first Gabonese player to appear in the Bundesliga.<sup id="cite_ref-Aubameyang_hat-trick_has_Dortmund_flying_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aubameyang_hat-trick_has_Dortmund_flying-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 27 November, he scored his first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> goal in a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage of the 2013–14 competition</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He later took a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> against <a href="/wiki/TSV_1860_Munich" title="TSV 1860 Munich">1860 Munich</a> that propelled Dortmund into the next round of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_DFB-Pokal" title="2013–14 DFB-Pokal">2013–14 DFB-Pokal</a>, finishing the year with 13 league goals and 16 goals in all competitions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315:_Second_DFL-Supercup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15:_Second_DFL-Supercup">2014–15: Second DFL-Supercup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2014–15: Second DFL-Supercup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_(BVB).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg/170px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="113" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg/255px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg/340px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%28BVB%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="2000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_(BVB).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang (left) playing for Borussia Dortmund in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 13 August 2014, Aubameyang assisted Borussia Dortmund's first goal and scored the second goal in a 2–0 victory over Bayern Munich in the <a href="/wiki/2014_DFL-Supercup" title="2014 DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Spider_Man_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spider_Man-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> After scoring the goal, he celebrated by putting on a <a href="/wiki/Spider-Man" title="Spider-Man">Spider-Man</a> mask.<sup id="cite_ref-Spider_Man_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spider_Man-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In Dortmund's next match, a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Stuttgarter_Kickers" title="Stuttgarter Kickers">Stuttgarter Kickers</a> in the first round of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_DFB-Pokal" title="2014–15 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a>, Aubameyang scored two-second-half goals and provided the assist for <a href="/wiki/Adri%C3%A1n_Ramos" title="Adrián Ramos">Adrián Ramos</a>' goal.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 13 September, Aubameyang scored his first <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Bundesliga" title="2014–15 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> goal of the season, netting Dortmund's final goal of their 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/SC_Freiburg" title="SC Freiburg">SC Freiburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Aubameyang scored Dortmund's second goal in a 2–0 win over future club <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in the first group match of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang ended his second season in Dortmund with 25 goals from 46 appearances, including one in the <a href="/wiki/2015_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2015 DFB-Pokal Final">2015 DFB-Pokal Final</a>, where Dortmund were defeated 3–1 by <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">VfL Wolfsburg</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Berlin)" title="Olympiastadion (Berlin)">Olympiastadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316:_League_runner-up"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16:_League_runner-up">2015–16: League runner-up</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2015–16: League runner-up">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 31 July 2015, Aubameyang signed a new contract to last until 2020, saying, "Every part of me wants to be here and I have never wanted to leave."<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> On 20 August, he scored a brace as Dortmund came from 0–3 down to win 3–4 at <a href="/wiki/Odds_BK" title="Odds BK">Odds BK</a> in the first leg of their Europa League <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Europa_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Play-off_round" class="mw-redirect" title="2015–16 UEFA Europa League qualifying phase and play-off round">play-off</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> By scoring in Dortmund's 1–1 draw with <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">1899 Hoffenheim</a> on 23 September, Aubameyang became the first player in Bundesliga history to score in each of his team's opening six matches of a season.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He later extended this record to eight matches, scoring in the team's next two fixtures against <a href="/wiki/SV_Darmstadt_98" title="SV Darmstadt 98">Darmstadt 98</a> and Bayern Munich, before failing to score for the first time in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Bundesliga" title="2015–16 Bundesliga">Bundesliga season</a> in a 2–0 win at <a href="/wiki/1._FSV_Mainz_05" title="1. FSV Mainz 05">Mainz 05</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 October, Aubameyang scored a hat-trick in a <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Gabala_FK" title="Gabala FK">Gabala</a> of Azerbaijan.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored another hat-trick in a 5–1 defeat of Augsburg at the <a href="/wiki/Westfalenstadion" title="Westfalenstadion">Westfalenstadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 8 November, Aubameyang scored the winning goal for Dortmund in a 3–2 <a href="/wiki/Revierderby" title="Revierderby">Revierderby</a> victory over rivals <a href="/wiki/FC_Schalke_04" title="FC Schalke 04">FC Schalke 04</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> At the halfway stage of the Bundesliga season, Aubameyang was the league's top scorer with 18 goals from 17 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 30 January 2016, Aubameyang scored his 19th and 20th league goals of the season to give Dortmund a 2–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Ingolstadt_04" title="FC Ingolstadt 04">FC Ingolstadt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang reached 30 goals in all competitions in a 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a> in the quarter-final of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_DFB-Pokal" title="2015–16 DFB-Pokal">2015–16 DFB-Pokal</a>. In addition to scoring himself, he assisted the side's other two goals scored by Marco Reus and <a href="/wiki/Henrikh_Mkhitaryan" title="Henrikh Mkhitaryan">Henrikh Mkhitaryan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 10 March 2016, Aubameyang scored for Borussia in their 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Europa_League#Round_of_16" title="2015–16 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League Round of 16</a> first-leg. A week later, he scored both goals in the 2–1 second-leg victory at <a href="/wiki/White_Hart_Lane" title="White Hart Lane">White Hart Lane</a>, taking him to 35 goals for the season.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In scoring two goals in a 5–1 win against VfL Wolfsburg on 30 April, Aubameyang reached 25 goals in the Bundesliga season, thus ending as the league's second-top scorer behind <a href="/wiki/Robert_Lewandowski" title="Robert Lewandowski">Robert Lewandowski</a> of Bayern Munich.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317:_Bundesliga_top_goalscorer_and_DFB-Pokal"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17:_Bundesliga_top_goalscorer_and_DFB-Pokal">2016–17: Bundesliga top goalscorer and DFB-Pokal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2016–17: Bundesliga top goalscorer and DFB-Pokal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Aubameyang170727.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Aubameyang170727.jpg/170px-Aubameyang170727.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Aubameyang170727.jpg/255px-Aubameyang170727.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Aubameyang170727.jpg/340px-Aubameyang170727.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3323" data-file-height="4985" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Aubameyang170727.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang training with Borussia Dortmund in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Aubameyang began his <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Bundesliga" title="2016–17 Bundesliga">2016–17 season</a> in the Bundesliga with a double against Mainz 05 on 27 August in a 2–1 victory, while also scoring twice against VfL Wolfsburg on 20 September. Aubameyang scored three days later against recently promoted SC Freiburg, bringing his season total to 5, into a tie atop the scoring charts with Lewandowski early in the season. Following an injury to <a href="/wiki/Marcel_Schmelzer" title="Marcel Schmelzer">Marcel Schmelzer</a>, Aubameyang wore the captain's armband for Dortmund for the first time on 22 October, also scoring a goal in the 3–3 draw at FC Ingolstadt.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang also got off to an excellent start in Dortmund's <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> group stage matches, scoring in each of their first leg matches as Dortmund were joint top of their group with <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>. However, Aubameyang was left out of the squad by <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Tuchel" title="Thomas Tuchel">Thomas Tuchel</a> for their return leg against <a href="/wiki/Sporting_CP" title="Sporting CP">Sporting CP</a> on 2 November due to an "internal issue".<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> It turned out that he received a one-game suspension for breaking club rules, by traveling to <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a> instead of staying in Dortmund.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Expected to return that weekend at <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>, Aubameyang exploded with a four-goal performance in a 5–2 victory, their first in five tries in the Bundesliga, while also assisting <a href="/wiki/Ousmane_Demb%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Ousmane Dembélé">Ousmane Dembélé</a> for Dortmund's final goal.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 November, Aubameyang scored the only goal of a 1–0 win over Bayern Munich at the Westfalenstadion. This was Dortmund's first Klassiker victory in the league since April 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On 7 December, Aubameyang scored Borussia's first goal in a 2–2 comeback draw with Real Madrid at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernabéu Stadium">Santiago Bernabéu Stadium</a> to secure qualification to the next stage as group winners.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 16 December, Aubameyang scored his 100th goal for Borussia Dortmund in a 2–2 draw away to 1899 Hoffenheim.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 March 2017, Aubameyang passed 20 Bundesliga goals for the second consecutive season with two goals in a 6–2 defeat of Bayer Leverkusen.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he scored a hat-trick in a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">Benfica</a> to put Dortmund into the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Quarter-final" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">quarter-finals</a> of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On 20 May, Aubameyang scored twice in Borussia's final day defeat of <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> to end the season as the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Bundesliga_top_scorers" title="List of Bundesliga top scorers">Bundesliga's top scorer</a> with 31 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2017_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2017 DFB-Pokal Final">final</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_DFB-Pokal" title="2016–17 DFB-Pokal">2016–17 DFB-Pokal</a> on 27 May 2017 he scored the winning goal, a penalty, as Dortmund beat <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arsenal">Arsenal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Arsenal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 31 January 2018, Aubameyang signed for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club, <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, for a then-club-record fee,<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> reported to be £56&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318:_Debut_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18:_Debut_season">2017–18: Debut season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2017–18: Debut season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_(28084398318).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg/170px-25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg/255px-25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg/340px-25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_%2828084398318%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1767" data-file-height="2653" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:25_Merci_Ars%C3%A8ne_-_Celebrating_Aubameyang%27s_goal_(28084398318).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang (left) celebrating a goal in Arsène Wenger's last home game as Arsenal manager, 2018</div></div></div>
<p>On 3 February, Aubameyang made his debut for Arsenal against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> in the Premier League in a 5–1 home victory, scoring the team's fourth goal, chipping the ball over a grounded <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Pickford" title="Jordan Pickford">Jordan Pickford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> After missing the Europa League matches against <a href="/wiki/%C3%96stersunds_FK" title="Östersunds FK">Östersunds FK</a> for the Gunners due to being cup-tied, Aubameyang registered his first away goal for the club in the team's 2–1 away defeat to <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang registered his first assist for the team, setting up Henrikh Mkhitaryan's goal in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>, Aubameyang also scored the Gunners' second goal (which was assisted by Mkhitaryan), rounding the goalkeeper.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang kept up his fine goalscoring form by scoring twice in Arsenal's 3–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>. Aubameyang's goals against Stoke (one of which was also his first converted penalty for the club) made him the first player to score five times in his first six games for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> He netted his second brace for Arsenal, in manager <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Arsène Wenger">Arsène Wenger</a>'s final home game for the club, opening and closing the scoring, whilst also assisting <a href="/wiki/Alex_Iwobi" title="Alex Iwobi">Alex Iwobi</a>'s goal, in an eventual 5–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang followed this up by scoring the only goal in Arsenal's 1–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Huddersfield_Town_A.F.C." title="Huddersfield Town A.F.C.">Huddersfield Town</a>. Aubameyang ended the season with ten goals and four assists in thirteen Premier League games and was the last goalscorer for Arsenal under Arsène Wenger.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319:_Premier_League_Golden_Boot"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19:_Premier_League_Golden_Boot">2018–19: Premier League Golden Boot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2018–19: Premier League Golden Boot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Aubameyang scored his first goal of the new season in a 3–2 away win over <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Cardiff City">Cardiff City</a> on 2 September 2018. After a flick from <a href="/wiki/Alexandre_Lacazette" title="Alexandre Lacazette">Alexandre Lacazette</a>, Aubameyang took a touch before curling the ball past the Cardiff goalkeeper. Aubameyang's strike from outside the box ended his personal run of 76 consecutive goals from inside the box in club football and was also his 150th goal in league football.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang made his European debut for Arsenal, in the 4–2 home win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Vorskla_Poltava" title="FC Vorskla Poltava">Vorskla Poltava</a>, scoring two goals, before being substituted for <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut Özil">Mesut Özil</a> in the 57th minute. Aubameyang's goals meant that he had been directly involved in 12 goals in 10 appearances for Arsenal at the <a href="/wiki/Emirates_Stadium" title="Emirates Stadium">Emirates Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> By October 2018, Aubameyang had tallied 16 goals in Premier League play since joining Arsenal in February. According to Opta statistics, that gave him a minutes per goal ratio of 104.6, which set the record for the best minutes per goal ratio in Premier League history (minimum 10 goals).<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang became the first player to reach 10 goals in the Premier League that season, following a brace in Arsenal's 4–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> in the <a href="/wiki/North_London_derby" title="North London derby">North London derby</a> on 2 December. Aubameyang scored the Gunners' opening goal from the penalty spot and later curled a shot past <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Lloris" title="Hugo Lloris">Hugo Lloris</a> in the second-half; he also grabbed an assist for Arsenal's fourth goal, which was <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Torreira" title="Lucas Torreira">Lucas Torreira</a>'s first goal for the club. The victory took Arsenal above Tottenham in the Premier League on goal difference.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang scored his first Arsenal hat-trick in the club's 4–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> on 9 May 2019. Aubameyang also set up the Gunners' second goal, scored by Alexandre Lacazette. Aubameyang's hat-trick meant that Arsenal reached the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Europa League Final">Europa League final</a>, making it the club's second European final in thirteen years.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> It also saw him become the first Arsenal player to score a hat-trick in the semi-finals of a European competition.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang finished the season with two goals in a 3–1 away win at Burnley, meaning he ended the season sharing the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Golden_Boot" title="Premier League Golden Boot">Premier League Golden Boot</a> title with Liverpool's <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sadio_Man%C3%A9" title="Sadio Mané">Sadio Mané</a>, on 22 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He played the full 90 minutes in Arsenal's 4–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in the Europa League, failing to make a significant impact as the result meant Arsenal missed out on Champions League qualification.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_FA_Cup_win"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20:_FA_Cup_win">2019–20: FA Cup win</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2019–20: FA Cup win">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 11 August 2019, Aubameyang scored his and Arsenal's first goal of the season in their 1–0 opening match victory over <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> at <a href="/wiki/St_James%27_Park" title="St James&#39; Park">St James' Park</a>, in which he demonstrated perfect technique to cushion a cross from <a href="/wiki/Ainsley_Maitland-Niles" title="Ainsley Maitland-Niles">Ainsley Maitland-Niles</a>, to slot the ball past <a href="/wiki/Martin_D%C3%BAbravka" title="Martin Dúbravka">Martin Dúbravka</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> hailing the strike as "a moment of genius".<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang scored his first home goal of the campaign in Arsenal's next game, a 2–1 win over Burnley on 17 August. Aubameyang scored what turned out to be the winning goal, following an assist from <a href="/wiki/Dani_Ceballos" title="Dani Ceballos">Dani Ceballos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang scored his first European goal of the season on 19 September against <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>, as Arsenal won 3–0 away from home on matchday 1.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang's five goals in September, including equalizers against Tottenham and <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and the winner against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>, saw him named the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a>, beating the likes of Liverpool's <a href="/wiki/Trent_Alexander-Arnold" title="Trent Alexander-Arnold">Trent Alexander-Arnold</a>, Tottenham's <a href="/wiki/Son_Heung-min" title="Son Heung-min">Son Heung-min</a> and Manchester City duo <a href="/wiki/Kevin_De_Bruyne" title="Kevin De Bruyne">Kevin De Bruyne</a> and <a href="/wiki/Riyad_Mahrez" title="Riyad Mahrez">Riyad Mahrez</a> to the award.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 November 2019, after <a href="/wiki/Granit_Xhaka" title="Granit Xhaka">Granit Xhaka</a> was stripped of the Arsenal captaincy following his angry reaction to getting booed by the Arsenal supporters during their <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> game against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> head coach <a href="/wiki/Unai_Emery" title="Unai Emery">Unai Emery</a> confirmed that Aubameyang would take over as the new Arsenal captain.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 December, following the dismissal of Emery, Aubameyang scored both goals in Arsenal's eventual 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a> in interim head coach <a href="/wiki/Freddie_Ljungberg" title="Freddie Ljungberg">Freddie Ljungberg</a>'s first game in charge. Aubameyang's first goal (a penalty) had to be retaken, after <a href="/wiki/Video_assistant_referee" title="Video assistant referee">VAR</a> discovered there to be encroachment in the penalty area. Aubameyang's first effort was kept out by goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Tim_Krul" title="Tim Krul">Tim Krul</a>, however, his second effort (the same side as his previous attempt), was successfully converted.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang scored in Arsenal's 1–1 draw with Crystal Palace on 11 January 2020, but was also sent off for a late challenge on Palace midfielder <a href="/wiki/Max_Meyer_(footballer)" title="Max Meyer (footballer)">Max Meyer</a>. Aubameyang was originally given a yellow card for the tackle by referee <a href="/wiki/Paul_Tierney_(referee)" title="Paul Tierney (referee)">Paul Tierney</a>, however the card was eventually upgraded to a red card, by the <a href="/wiki/Video_Assistant_Referee" class="mw-redirect" title="Video Assistant Referee">VAR</a>, resulting in Aubameyang's first-ever red card for the Gunners and would mean that the striker would miss Arsenal's next three matches against <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_United_F.C." title="Sheffield United F.C.">Sheffield United</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and Arsenal's <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> tie against <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 February, in Arsenal's Europa League second leg round of 32 match against <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a> and with the aggregate score tied at 1–1, Aubameyang's scissor kick goal in extra time allowed his side to equalize the match and lead the tie on aggregate. However, following a 119th-minute goal by Olympiacos that meant Arsenal would be heading out of the competition, Aubameyang missed an open shot from five yards out in the last seconds of the match that would have seen his side through.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Following Arsenal's elimination, Aubameyang apologized for and lamented his miss, stating, "I feel very, very bad. It can happen but I do not know how I missed this chance. I was tired, I had some cramps but it is not an excuse."<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the resumption of the league in the wake of the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, Aubameyang did not score or assist in the first three Premier League games after the restart for Arsenal, but eventually netted a brace on 1 July against Norwich City in a 4–0 rout. Aubameyang's first goal was his 50th in the league for Arsenal, making him the quickest player to reach 50 goals for the club in the Premier League era, having achieved the feat in just 79 league appearances, four games quicker than all-time club goalscorer <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a>, and also became the sixth fastest to 50 in the Premier League, behind <a href="/wiki/Andy_Cole" title="Andy Cole">Andy Cole</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alan_Shearer" title="Alan Shearer">Alan Shearer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ruud_van_Nistelrooy" title="Ruud van Nistelrooy">Ruud van Nistelrooy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a> and Mohamed Salah.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Aubameyang also assisted the Gunners' second goal, which was scored by Granit Xhaka.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> He ended the season with 22 league goals, one behind <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Vardy" title="Jamie Vardy">Jamie Vardy</a>, the winner of the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Golden_Boot" title="Premier League Golden Boot">Golden Boot</a>, and tied with <a href="/wiki/Danny_Ings" title="Danny Ings">Danny Ings</a> for second place.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 July, in their FA Cup semi-final against defending champions <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, Aubameyang scored both goals in a 2–0 win for Arsenal, sending them to the <a href="/wiki/2020_FA_Cup_Final" title="2020 FA Cup Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 1 August, he converted a penalty and scored the winner in the final, as Arsenal defeated <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> 2–1 and Aubameyang lifted his first trophy with the club, becoming the first African to win the FA Cup as a captain.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbc_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 29 August, Aubameyang scored a goal in normal time and the fifth and winning penalty in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">shoot-out</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020_FA_Community_Shield" title="2020 FA Community Shield">Community Shield</a>, after the game ended 1–1.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> On 12 September, he scored in the first league game of the new season the final goal of a 3–0 win away to <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> On 15 September, Aubameyang signed a new three-year contract with Arsenal.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> On 1 November, he scored a penalty in a 1–0 away win against Manchester United, to grant Arsenal their first Premier League win at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> since 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang scored two goals for Arsenal in their 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> on 18 January 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> However, he did not play in the club's next three matches, in order to tend to his ill mother.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 14 February, Aubameyang scored his first <a href="/wiki/List_of_Premier_League_hat-tricks" title="List of Premier League hat-tricks">Premier League hat-trick</a> in a 4–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds United</a>. This took him to 200 career goals across Europe's top five leagues.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> On 25 February, he scored two goals against Benfica in a 3–2 win to secure Arsenal a place in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> On March 14th 2021 Aubameyang was left out of the starting line up in the North London Derby againt Tottenham, the manager citing disciplinary reasons.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%E2%80%93_Gabon_national_football_team.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%E2%80%93_Gabon_national_football_team.jpg/170px-Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%E2%80%93_Gabon_national_football_team.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="183" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/61/Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%E2%80%93_Gabon_national_football_team.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="215" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang_%E2%80%93_Gabon_national_football_team.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Aubameyang playing for <a href="/wiki/Gabon_national_under-23_football_team" title="Gabon national under-23 football team">Gabon</a> against <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2012 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2012 Summer Olympics</a></div></div></div>
<p>Aubameyang was invited to play for <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_under-19_football_team" title="Italy national under-19 football team">Italy U19s</a> after a good season with Dijon, but he debuted for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">France under-21</a> team in February 2009 in a friendly match against Tunisia.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang was also eligible to play for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> because he has Spanish nationality. He decided to represent Gabon because his father once captained the team, but he maintains close relationship with Spain and dreams to play in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 25 March 2009, Aubameyang was selected for the <a href="/wiki/Gabon_national_football_team" title="Gabon national football team">Gabon national team</a><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> and made his debut for the squad. He scored his first goal in a 2–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Morocco_national_football_team" title="Morocco national football team">Morocco</a>, then scored a goal each in friendly matches against <a href="/wiki/Benin_national_football_team" title="Benin national football team">Benin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Togo_national_football_team" title="Togo national football team">Togo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Senegal_national_football_team" title="Senegal national football team">Senegal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang was a key member of the Gabon national side that reached the quarter-finals of the <a href="/wiki/2012_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2012 Africa Cup of Nations">2012 Africa Cup of Nations</a> as co-hosts of the competition. He netted three goals in total, finishing the tournament as one of the top scorers. On 5 February 2012, he set up the opening goal for his team and hit the post in the quarter-final against <a href="/wiki/Mali_national_football_team" title="Mali national football team">Mali</a>. However, the match ended 1–1 after <a href="/wiki/Extra_time" class="mw-redirect" title="Extra time">extra time</a> and Aubameyang had his penalty saved in the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout" title="Penalty shootout">shootout</a> to decide the game.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2012, Aubameyang represented <a href="/wiki/Gabon_national_under-23_football_team" title="Gabon national under-23 football team">Gabon</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2012 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2012 Summer Olympics</a> in London. He scored in the team's opening game against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_under-23_football_team" title="Switzerland national under-23 football team">Switzerland</a>, which was Gabon's first-ever Olympic goal, and would also prove to be Gabon's only goal of the tournament. They were eliminated in the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 June 2013, Aubameyang scored a hat-trick of penalty kicks in Gabon's 4–1 <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CAF_Second_Round" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification – CAF Second Round">qualifying</a> win over <a href="/wiki/Niger_national_football_team" title="Niger national football team">Niger</a>. He then scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Burkina_Faso_national_football_team" title="Burkina Faso national football team">Burkina Faso</a> in the 2015 Africa Cup of Nations Qualification.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Aubameyang <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captained</a> Gabon at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">2015 Africa Cup of Nations</a>, scoring the team's opening goal of the tournament in their 2–0 win over Burkina Faso on 17 January 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> He also scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Mali_national_football_team" title="Mali national football team">Mali</a> on 25 March 2015. He is Gabon's highest goalscorer. He rejected a callup for a pivotal World Cup qualifier at home to the Ivory Coast, which they lost 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Aubameyang was born in <a href="/wiki/Laval,_Mayenne" title="Laval, Mayenne">Laval</a>, France.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> He is the son of former Gabonese international footballer <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Aubameyang" title="Pierre Aubameyang">Pierre Aubameyang</a> and younger half-brother of <a href="/wiki/Catilina_Aubameyang" title="Catilina Aubameyang">Catilina</a> and <a href="/wiki/Willy_Aubameyang" title="Willy Aubameyang">Willy</a>, who have both played for Milan's youth teams.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> His mother is Spanish.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
He is married to Alysha Behague, the couple has two sons, Curtys and Pierre.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is multilingual and speaks French, English, Spanish, Italian, and German.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pierre-Emerick_Aubameyang&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
